ence-a-href-cite-note-endowment-2-2-a-sup-td-tr-tr-th-scope-row-style-padding-right-0-65em-budget-th-td-8-99-billion-2018-sup-id-cite-ref-3-class-reference-a-href-cite-note-3-3-a-sup-td-tr-tr-th-scope-row-style-padding-right-0-65em-a-href-wiki-university-president-class-mw-redirect-title-university-president-president-a-th-td-a-href-wiki-mark-schlissel-title-mark-schlissel-mark-schlissel-a-td-tr-tr-th-scope-row-style-padding-right-0-65em-a-href-wiki-provost-education-title-provost-education-provost-a-th-td-a-href-w-index-php-title-martin-philbert-action-edit-redlink-1-class-new-title-martin-philbert-page-does-not-exist-martin-philbert-a-td-tr-tr-th-scope-row-style-padding-right-0-65em-div-style-padding-0-1em-0-line-height-1-2em-academic-staff-div-th-td-6771-sup-id-cite-ref-umich2-4-0-class-reference-a-href-cite-note-umich2-4-4-a-sup-td-tr-tr-th-scope-row-style-padding-right-0-65em-div-style-padding-0-1em-0-line-height-1-2em-administrative-staff-div-th-td-18986-sup-id-cite-ref-umich1-5-0-class-reference-a-href-cite-note-umich1-5-5-a-sup-td-tr-tr-th-scope-row-style-padding-right-0-65em-students-th-td-46002-sup-id-cite-ref-enrollment-6-0-class-reference-a-href-cite-note-enrollment-6-6-a-sup-td-tr-tr-th-scope-row-style-padding-right-0-65em-a-href-wiki-undergraduate-education-title-undergraduate-education-undergraduates-a-th-td-29821-sup-id-cite-ref-enrollment-6-1-class-reference-a-href-cite-note-enrollment-6-6-a-sup-td-tr-tr-th-scope-row-style-padding-right-0-65em-a-href-wiki-postgraduate-education-title-postgraduate-education-postgraduates-a-th-td-16181-sup-id-cite-ref-enrollment-6-2-class-reference-a-href-cite-note-enrollment-6-6-a-sup-td-tr-tr-th-scope-row-style-padding-right-0-65em-location-th-td-class-adr-div-style-display-inline-class-locality-a-href-wiki-ann-arbor-michigan-title-ann-arbor-michigan-ann-arbor-a-div-div-style-display-inline-class-state-a-href-wiki-michigan-title-michigan-michigan-a-div-div-style-display-inline-class-country-name-united-states-div-br
